What is Player A's role? 'H' for human player, 'R' for robot player.
What is Player B's role? 'H' for human player, 'R' for robot player.

-----------------------------------------------------

Player A, you are going place Sally’s stash on the board. Make sure Player B isn’t looking!  For  each  stack,  type  the  coordinate  of  the  upper  left  side  of  the  stash, followed  by  either  H  (for  horizontal)  or  V  (for  vertical).  For  example,  M4H  would place a stackhorizontally starting at M4 and going to the right.You have 
1 Greenstacks that are 1x2
1 Purple stacks that are 1x3
2 Red stacks that are Super Stacks
2 Blue stacks that are Crazy Stacks

For  each  stack,  type  the  coordinate  of  the  upper  left  side  of  the  stash, followed  by  either  H  (for  horizontal)  or  V  (for  vertical).  For  example,  M4H  would place a stackhorizontally starting at M4 and going to the right.You have 
1 Greenstacks that are 1x2
1 Purple stacks that are 1x3
2 Red stacks that are Super Stacks
2 Blue stacks that are Crazy Stacks
